< Review>
I really admire and appreciate Dr. Nogueiro.  Before I met him recently, I went to a string of four dentists in the East Bay over about six years and handed over $10,000-$12,000 out of pocket to those idiots.  Every dentist seemed worse than the last one.  After all that my teeth were so messed up I could not even touch my front teeth together, everything hurt, I had big new dental problems and it looked like hell.  I woke up with headaches even with a mouthguard I made myself (one dentist could not make one that fit, and one just would never make me one).  Decay was not a big issue, this work was mostly replacements of old fillings and crowns.  I could tell you five or six very expensive horror stories that would, well, horrify you.  It would take pages.

Then luckily I found Dr. Nogueiro, courtesy of a referral from the best endodontist in the Bay Area, Dr. Nesari on Mission.  Dr. Nogueiro has done a full bite analysis with a cast he made and studied and is making many effective adjustments.  He fixed the crown problems, put in a great, comfortable bridge and is fixing the horrible mess on my front top teeth.  Instead of six or seven areas that hurt when I eat, I'm down to one and it's not bad.  He adjusts and I feel better.  It was hard for me at first to even tell him where it hurt, but he figured it out.  No pain at all, like zero, anymore the rest of the time (it's been years) and I am sleeping much better.  I feel better generally.  My mouth looks and feels so much better, I can't even tell you.  He also did me an emergency solid when some old bonding broke and I had a big event coming up.

So anyway, I didn't expect him to perform miracles on my messed up teeth but he kinda did anyway.  The man has skills and is innovative.  Plus he's really nice and made me cry from laughing (instead of from pain and terror) during the last appointment with a golf story.  Can't beat that.  His staff are good at their jobs and very sweet and efficient, it is a low stress visit.

I could not be more appreciative.

I should also mention it takes me 1.5 to 2 hours to travel to the city for an appointment via public transport, and I think he is out of my dental network, AND I DON'T CARE.  His skills are worth it. I feel that much better. Plus prices are really good, and that's important, too.  And the Mission district rocks, it's fun to walk around and eat lunch.< /Review>

<Text>Good tires and good service.
I've got the new tires for my 96 Jeep Gr Cherokee right before New Year 2015 and it was a very nice gift for me. Good tires, quick and professional service for the best price I could find. I bought four GoodYear Wrangler 235/75 R15 SR-A tires and I'm very satisfied with them. They look nice and they perform very well. The car became softer and essentially more stable on freeway and city driving. Off-road capability is also increased. Although rolling resistance is noticeably increased (because of softer and wider tires), the fuel mileage is not affected much (because of bigger diameter of the tire: 75% of 235 vs 75% of 225 which I had before). Got an online appointment for a a tire change 4 days in advance. Picked the tires I wanted and everything was going smoothly. Until I showed up, that is. I was then told they didn't have the tires I picked out. I was actually thinking it was just a logistics problem -- the tires didn't get there in time. It happens. Honest mistake. Excellent. William really took care of me like family. First of all I had all my brakes done a couple months ago...very satisfied, but this review is about my 2001 Toyota Solara engine job. William explained to me that no, I needed a valve job and that if it broke could ruin the whole engine. A valve job is not cheap but I said go ahead. 3 to 4 days later he called me to say it was finished but come to find out that the horrible noise wasn't from the valves, it was in the lower block of the engine and that wasn't good and I needed a new engine. Ugh!, right? He then told me he wasn't going to charge me a penny for the valve job, gave me a really great price for a new engine complete with rebuilt long block, new water pump, thermostat, timing belt and tentionser, and including labor. There were also a few minor things I asked him to do also like like a burnt out bulb, recharge air conditioner, he said he'd take care of those extras no charge. My car runs beautifully! Thank you Wil.</Text>
